Directory 2023

Connecticut Judicial Branch

www.jud.ct.gov

JDP-ES-190

Telecommunications Relay Service

TDD/TT Users:
Call 711 or 1-800-842-9710

Voice Callers:
Call 711 or 1-800-833-8134

The Connecticut Judicial Branch Directory is provided 
to you by the External Affairs Division and is published 
by the Commission on Official Legal Publications of 
the Information Technology Division. It is updated 
regularly and available online.

Cheryl MacDonald, Editor
(860) 757-2270

Photographs of historical items in the Roy Smith, Jr.  
Jury Assembly Room, Tolland Judicial District.

ITEM  
Appeal to Supreme Court or Appellate Court – entry 
fee, 52-259.
